@pytest.mark.test_p0
def test_I2_5_5(indigo2_obj, request, get_init_datetime, requires_sdktestapp, requires_wifi):
"""Verify on-demand kernel logging feature

Prerequisite: Wifi should be connected.
Automation prerequisite steps:
1. Install AOSPTestApp (if not already available)
2. Connect to Wifi
3. Open SDKTestApp MainActivity
4. Wait for SecureService to be connected and ApplianceManager bind with wlogging service

5. Execute following command to trigget kernel log upload
adb shell am broadcast -a com.whirlpool.wloggingservice.WLOGGING_INTENT -e com.whirlpool.wloggingservice.COMMAND UPLOAD_KERNEL_LOG

6. Look for file uploaded log in logcat.
yyyy-mm-dd hh:mm:ss <PID-PID>/com.whirlpool.ees.indigo2.wloggingservice D/AWSUtility: /sdcard/crashlog/<filename >.txt: File uploaded successfully

7. Verify kernel log file is uploaded to AWS S3 bucket whr-visioncloud-jupiter-dev → Kernel-Log → SAID→<filename>.txt .
"""
# get the test case number from the test case function name
test_case_no = get_test_case_no_for_report(request)
logging.info(test_case_no)
d_date, d_time = get_init_datetime
# Launch SDKTestApp and wait for secure service to connect
testactivity = "MainActivity"
indigo2_obj.run_apk_activity(_sdktest_activity + testactivity)
# Wait for Secureservice to be connected and ApplianceManager bind with wlogging service (connected)
keyword = "WLoggingServiceInterface: connnect: bound to WLoggingService"
ret_val, line = indigo2_obj.logcat_wait_keyword(keyword, d_date, d_time, 30)
#t.sleep(30)
cmd = " am broadcast -a com.whirlpool.wloggingservice.WLOGGING_INTENT -e com.whirlpool.wloggingservice.COMMAND UPLOAD_KERNEL_LOG"
result, err = indigo2_obj.shell_execute(cmd)
assert("Broadcast completed: result=0" in result)
#keyword = "_kernellogs.txt : File uploaded successfully"
'''
Kernel log uploaded successfully

'''
kword1 = "_kernellogs.txt : File uploaded successfully"
'''
This may happen when there is AWS connection issue (S3 issue).
